For the red object to fall and make contact with the floor, the sphere needs to impart enough energy through a collision to topple the tower. **Scene B:** This scene features a very tall and thin tower. The green sphere's impact will have a much greater chance of toppling this tower due to its high center of gravity and narrow base. **Scene C:** The tower here is sitting on a complex base with various levels and components. While this offers a degree of stability, it's also uneven and potentially prone to rocking or tilting.
